# Operation

## Overview

AR.IO Gateways are the interface between users and the Permaweb. Each Gateway acts like a "Permaweb Service Provider" and supports multiple, value-added, low-trust services for users and applications. The AR.IO HTTP API is served by all AR.IO Gateways, and is used by all Arweave clients looking to read, write, and query data. It supports the following capabilities:

- Seeding layer one transactions to the greater Arweave network
- Caching and serving chain and transaction data
- Resolving friendly names to transaction data with the Arweave Name System
- Indexing and querying layer one and two transactions
- Proxy for Arweave nodes serving the Arweave HTTP API

### Errors

The API uses standard HTTP status codes to indicate the success of failure of the API call

### Authentication

All inbound transactions to the Arweave network must contain a valid signature from an Arweave wallet with the appropriate amount of AR Tokens. At this time, clients are not required to sign their requests for outbound data from the Arweave network.

## Cache

Provides data from the AR.IO Gateway cache

### Transaction

Gets Transaction data

`/{txId}`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/dBSTUg33LAsC5ThFwiTXao873v34QNM_x-BvaaOK13E
```

Response

```
{"name":"Bananas.jpg","size":587828,"lastModifiedDate":1684980169000,"dataTxId":"h6sV7ST1gKAlRSvdOLoSiGg2nL2vZky_KYTj9M0GVS0","dataContentType":"image/jpeg"}
```

</details>

### Raw Transation

Gets the Raw data from a transaction, for example it can display the contents of an Arweave Manifest instead of directing your gateway to where the Manifest is pointing.

`/raw/{txId}`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/raw/GPOX8dgUpFpt8IVUyyfBMiPpfWZ9eXHZjNi42W4-_50
```

Response

```
{"manifest":"arweave/paths","version":"0.1.0","index":{"path":"index.html"},"paths":{"about.html":{"id":"fOAhaHRcaVzbMgmWAEdPncX-ZsKVZgrFOor2BOQkLU4"},"index.html":{"id":"M4TIc72VRXUPfFZOnmqL1CsLLzdMrpONNelpyoD31KI"},"style.css":{"id":"CvGTQ3YpFsOQ6Xh1hPhSnyTQFPa6TUpGFmGZsIwaZDU"},"script.js":{"id":"xR8THTsuYrSnEmXueECknpbipvDcCKqqCg79Thos_I4"},"home.html":{"id":"2SzIqpI_fWuxX0j-FYMfIVUXtf7de0aaQJvp39d12UU"},"deploy.html":{"id":"HPdPumduTm17_aWnD2VDeaXJJHc_eGD2QloP0Zc0Byk"},"hash.html":{"id":"0p6gssMZ3R9iDFScwD9JKcW9snWTw5rqHnr5o8JXYy4"},"paths.html":{"id":"6nCmNdMxfb9zMYsl3pwFzFQ-AFIPjhVC9W4ZRs4QH4c"},"update.html":{"id":"BNKaYC6zmeS7ABycqmhLcmEHQKXw4B5RtD-v3nZ2rdk"},"code.html":{"id":"LC08UXIjb4Lv64pVSI-pC7c_tY9L221Sb27xBP4Q-qc"}}}
```

</details>

## Network

This group of endpoints can provide information on Arweave nodes, peers, and network status. Use "GET" requests for all queries.

### Network information

Provides information on the Arweave network and your Gateway, including version and release numbers, block height, current transaction, peers, and latency.

`/` or `/info`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/info
```

Response

```
{
    "network":"arweave.N.1",
    "version":5,"release":65,"height":1236124,"current":"QwOoSCP_BEwI0e1hGOU1VRZ2kwrF_lnlcGFLIn8g0hEpDcICtDXzFlVmEZlhgVz4",
    "blocks":1236125,
    "peers":90,
    "queue_length":0,
    "node_state_latency":1
}
```

</details>

### Peer information

Provides an array of peers your Gateway is connected to.

`/peers`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/peers
```

Response

```
[
    "159.69.65.150:1984","162.55.176.19:1984","109.120.235.125:10011","23.22.197.174:1984","3.14.99.13:1984","198.244.165.146:1984","144.76.176.26:1984","34.92.74.22:1984","139.59.19.218:1984"
]
```

</details>

### Network Block Height

Provides the current Arweave Network block height

`/height`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/height
```

Response

```
1236128
```

</details>

## Pricing

### Upload

Provides the price (in Winston) for uploading data (in bytes) to the network.

`/price/{size}`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/price/5000000
```

Response

```
4191625910
```

</details>

### Transfer and Upload

Provides the price (in Winston) for transferring AR to a new wallet in order to pay for an upload

`/price/{size}/target`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/price/5000000/target
```

Response

```
16192017846
```

</details>

## Wallets

Provides information about public Arweave Wallet Addresses

### Balance

Provides the current balance of AR (in Winston) of the given address

`/wallet/{address}/balance`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/wallet/cF0H0SKdnaDTqWKY9iJKBktTpdEWgb3GnlndE7ABv0Q/balance
```

Response

```
49708373893732
```

</details>

### Last Transaction

Provides the TX ID for the last transaction completed

`/wallet/{address}/last_tx`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/wallet/cF0H0SKdnaDTqWKY9iJKBktTpdEWgb3GnlndE7ABv0Q/last_tx
```

Response

```
49708373893732
```

</details>

## Blocks

Provides current or historical Arweave Block Information

### Current Block

Provides information on the current block

`/current_block` or `/block/current`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/current_block
```

### Specific Block

Provides information on a specific block height.

`/block/height/{height}`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/block/height/1984
```

Response


### Get Block by Hash

`/block/hash/{hash}`

Request

```
https://arweave.net/block/hash/CA_J-ci5ePeg7_I7YS3Be66MGrhA_DM6nzS5azlhKpkc7yOZ0p-2sf6OsR6slNr7
```

Provides information on Arweave Transactions.

### Pending

Provides array of pending transactions

`/tx/pending`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/tx/pending
```

Response

```
["A8lCZPTAwuBY5HfuVbFJsJ4F0KB205_UEO8XNJ9ArSU","hTLgucGtdEfWqiWYqqaEQB97o8NyN6zA6cXTHX8pI8E","aH-Qk6q4LZ0K1GLB1rmX8YvxB9g7rLsekwR79jqxCOM","RuMRsMMbezwBo-5HjqLHG8guex8fu18o5_XHI0TxZsY","C05c6xfq1m7z-kdIyVwaVftIj0N8AcQc9XB9h5NYgHQ","l_eODdrwQqjgzcDUr6NE-tt2V4ikYTTPXE9Jz3FNSGU","p4IPTJPCrS7wlB3p7s1o-JM6npTDm3QEv2CTHZXD7JU","bKlMQOoy1N4J9ATvjlytAuXuhm_Tkm_vy9CpabkMUv0","ADsLCxBfsWfEZeR62MTMnw1i54R_JA_7woeEh5sFZv8","P8lhRilLZyPdnn70yaphbfHM5IxtOneZvK3gUSPXG7E","ecoEWsHW1jbuQriKeASvrPEzS7rJ2Mzajf4pzGyiO0s","mswc2wOm4tcevSBRqg840RTBLebVI2w5MjuDGXvCX8E","UC9RyAztDfMJCx7HlZ2z4ykOUJzidqRE1T0v-f_6BPU","JGmJPI7n0qHk7RCzEvKCXWbEBCrazAFGrL8_WiJFF1U","NVUYFvLdubJ5gUPfPy3jZvws6KZ1yL2mD7wwKdXjdOE","-rnYkfarerxLtfLsXzAkU6On_T0IQyarO7Zn5rP7Rl4","8j6o4fqp-vl6_GYMbFibAf5ajzwTf-Swgd_eovIGwp0","Os19pbfIynoDZCR9JCYDmC1gQxc6x4iY0N_JIX9N7Rg","WQtP7nfqFByTR3ZXF3O7a1Ueb9X9bObTj6N-OiDjxXs","lPk88ilQk7PSeHD-4M8G49CgMQ30RlkVjEv0-ENbv80","lKDFDPRo1_VXZNiXMsxcMp5u_fbSGuJEri-FyO3bu0g","Zkx8Jrk__oNSHdUyN1WAVBLdIIzc2oAVZvDSciOyfn0","Ic6ucH_LZv1-3lrGgvXDJoMh8ZOAz2JyRrnsYRuVE20","JaVM0GT37c0P015cCR24ltYcsRH7x8ubniXzoAojh1Y","MtCURfaU3mvnOObVkVEVUJv6LlaCRoHrbQskxCdE_Bg","ur6r8PS2RC3J0A3hQyq4IrON4QJHJQxkHZOGkpZ_Mqk","hL_ZItvhslgS4s_mY-o6_TH78DyEvIqzaEjRfKuGQaI","k2pFW1ysC9QyX9aPeEHcr1yiO8JVi06PUz7L7y-Il4U","8XYuS9SQ0SLkuzZWDWlW58D0KHeEkrChwPdh0ZnTYWo"]
```

</details>
</details>

### Transaction

Provides information on a transaction based on a txId

`/tx/{txId}`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/tx/A8lCZPTAwuBY5HfuVbFJsJ4F0KB205_UEO8XNJ9ArSU
```

<details><summary>Response</summary>


### Offset

Provides information on the size and offset of a given txId

`tx/{txId}/offset`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/tx/A8lCZPTAwuBY5HfuVbFJsJ4F0KB205_UEO8XNJ9ArSU/offset
```

Response

```
{"size":"17281162","offset":"146788128412032"}
```

</details>

### Status

Provides the status of a transaction based on its txId

`/tx/{txId}/status`

<details><summary>Exemple</summary>

Request

```
https://bobinstein.com/tx/A8lCZPTAwuBY5HfuVbFJsJ4F0KB205_UEO8XNJ9ArSU/status
```

Response

```
{"block_height":1236198,"block_indep_hash":"BiNSjNDLURchLF34-J0pEPcyPkWwAGslY_ziQn235s2RoyLlveVso_iMPkZvgU4w","number_of_confirmations":14}
```

</details>
</details>

## Chunks

Get existing chunk offset information

`/chunk/{offset}`

<details><summary>Example</summary>

Request

```
https://arweave.net/chunk/146788128412032
```

